     1^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mIDENTIFICATION[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mDIVISION[39;49;00m.$
     2^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mPROGRAM-ID[39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mOCic[39;49;00m.$
     3^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
     4^I[37m      ** This program provides a Textual User Interface (TUI) to the **[39;49;00m$
     5^I[37m      ** process of compiling and (optionally) executing an OpenCOBOL**[39;49;00m$
     6^I[37m      ** program.                                                    **[39;49;00m$
     7^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
     8^I[37m      ** This programs execution syntax is as follows:               **[39;49;00m$
     9^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
    10^I[37m      ** ocic <program-path-and-filename> [ <switch>... ]            **[39;49;00m$
    11^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
    12^I[37m      ** Once executed, a display screen will be presented showing   **[39;49;00m$
    13^I[37m      ** the compilation options that will be used.  The user will   **[39;49;00m$
    14^I[37m      ** have the opportunity to change options, specify new ones    **[39;49;00m$
    15^I[37m      ** and specify any program execution arguments to be used if   **[39;49;00m$
    16^I[37m      ** you select the "Execute" option.  When you press the Enter  **[39;49;00m$
    17^I[37m      ** key the program will be compiled.                           **[39;49;00m$
    18^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
    19^I[37m      ** The SCREEN SECTION contains an image of the screen.         **[39;49;00m$
    20^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
    21^I[37m      ** The "010-Parse-Args" section in the PROCEDURE DIVISION has  **[39;49;00m$
    22^I[37m      ** documentation on switches and their function.               **[39;49;00m$
    23^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
    24^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
    25^I[37m      ** AUTHOR:       GARY L. CUTLER                                **[39;49;00m$
    26^I[37m      **               CutlerGL@gmail.com                            **[39;49;00m$
    27^I[37m      **               Copyright (C) 2009-2010, Gary L. Cutler, GPL  **[39;49;00m$
    28^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
    29^I[37m      ** DATE-WRITTEN: June 14, 2009                                 **[39;49;00m$
    30^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
    31^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
    32^I[37m      ** Note: Depending on which extended DISPLAY handler you're    **[39;49;00m$
    33^I[37m      **       using (PDCurses, Curses, ...), you may need to un-    **[39;49;00m$
    34^I[37m      **       comment any source lines tagged with "SCROLL" in cols **[39;49;00m$
    35^I[37m      **       1-6 in order to have error messages scroll properly   **[39;49;00m$
    36^I[37m      **       in the OCic shell window.                             **[39;49;00m$
    37^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
    38^I[37m      **  DATE  CHANGE DESCRIPTION                                   **[39;49;00m$
    39^I[37m      ** ====== ==================================================== **[39;49;00m$
    40^I[37m      ** GC0609 Don't display compiler messages file if compilation  **[39;49;00m$
    41^I[37m      **        Is successful.  Also don't display messages if the   **[39;49;00m$
    42^I[37m      **        output file is busy (just put a message on the       **[39;49;00m$
    43^I[37m      **        screen, leave the OC screen up & let the user fix    **[39;49;00m$
    44^I[37m      **        the problem & resubmit.                              **[39;49;00m$
    45^I[37m      ** GC0709 When 'EXECUTE' is selected, a 'FILE BUSY' error will **[39;49;00m$
    46^I[37m      **        still cause the (old) executable to be launched.     **[39;49;00m$
    47^I[37m      **        Also, the 'EXTRA SWITCHES' field is being ignored.   **[39;49;00m$
    48^I[37m      **        Changed the title bar to lowlighted reverse video &  **[39;49;00m$
    49^I[37m      **        the message area to highlighted reverse-video.       **[39;49;00m$
    50^I[37m      ** GC0809 Add a SPACE in from of command-line args when        **[39;49;00m$
    51^I[37m      **        executing users program.  Add a SPACE after the      **[39;49;00m$
    52^I[37m      **        -ftraceall switch when building cobc command.        **[39;49;00m$
    53^I[37m      ** GC0909 Convert to work on Cygwin/Linux as well as MinGW     **[39;49;00m$
    54^I[37m      ** GC0310 Virtualized the key codes for S-F1 thru S-F7 as they **[39;49;00m$
    55^I[37m      **        differ depending upon whether PDCurses or NCurses is **[39;49;00m$
    56^I[37m      **        being used.                                          **[39;49;00m$
    57^I[37m      ** GC0410 Introduced the cross-reference and source listing    **[39;49;00m$
    58^I[37m      **        features.  Also fixed a bug in @EXTRA switch proces- **[39;49;00m$
    59^I[37m      **        sing where garbage will result if more than the      **[39;49;00m$
    60^I[37m      **        @EXTRA switch is specified.                          **[39;49;00m$

   242^I[37m      *> Here is the layout of the OCic screen.[39;49;00m$
   243^I[37m      *>[39;49;00m$
   244^I[37m      *> Note that this program can utilize the traditional PC line-drawing characters,[39;49;00m$
   245^I[37m      *> if they are available.[39;49;00m$
   246^I[37m      *>[39;49;00m$
   247^I[37m      *> If this program is run on Windows, it must run with codepage 437 activated to[39;49;00m$
   248^I[37m      *> display the line-drawing characters.  With a native Windows build or a[39;49;00m$
   249^I[37m      *> Windows/MinGW build, one could use the command "chcp 437" to set that codepage[39;49;00m$
   250^I[37m      *> for display within a Windows console window (that should be the default, though).[39;49;00m$
   251^I[37m      *> With a Windows/Cygwin build, set the environment variable CYGWIN to a value of[39;49;00m$
   252^I[37m      *> "codepage:oem" (this cannot be done from within the program though - you will[39;49;00m$
   253^I[37m      *> have to use the "Computer/Advanced System Settings/Environment Variables" (Vista or[39;49;00m$
   254^I[37m      *> Windows 7) function to define the variable.  XP Users: use "My Computer/Properties/[39;49;00m$
   255^I[37m      *> Advanced/Environment Variables".[39;49;00m$
   256^I[37m      *>[39;49;00m$
   257^I[37m      *> To use OCic without the line-drawing characters, comment-out the first set of[39;49;00m$
   258^I[37m      *> 78 "LD" items and uncomment the second.[39;49;00m$
   259^I[37m      *>[39;49;00m$
   260^I[37m      *> The following sample screen layout shows how the screen looks with line-drawing[39;49;00m$
   261^I[37m      *> characters disabled.[39;49;00m$

   545^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                   [39;49;00m[31mMSG[39;49;00m[37m    [39;49;00m[34mBY[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mFSM-Msg[39;49;00m.$
   546^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mMOVE[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSPACES[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mOutput-Message[39;49;00m$
   547^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mIF[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mFSM-Status[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[34m35[39;49;00m$
   548^I[34m               [39;49;00m[34mDISPLAY[39;49;00m$
   549^I[34m                   [39;49;00m[33m'File not found: "'[39;49;00m$
   550^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[32mTRIM[39;49;00m([31mFile-Name[39;49;00m,[34mTRAILING[39;49;00m)$
   551^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[33m'"'[39;49;00m$
   552^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mEND-DISPLAY[39;49;00m$
   553^I[34m          [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mELSE[39;49;00m$
   554^I[34m              [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mDISPLAY[39;49;00m$
   555^I[34m                   [39;49;00m[33m'Error accessing file: "'[39;49;00m$
   556^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[32mTRIM[39;49;00m([31mFile-Name[39;49;00m,[34mTRAILING[39;49;00m)$
   557^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[33m'"'[39;49;00m$
   558^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mEND-DISPLAY[39;49;00m$
   559^I[34m          [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mEND-IF[39;49;00m$
   560^I[34m          [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mGOBACK[39;49;00m$
   561^I[34m           [39;49;00m.$
   562^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mEND[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mDECLARATIVES[39;49;00m.$
   563^I[37m      /[39;49;00m$
   564^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m000[39;49;00m-[31mMain[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mSECTION[39;49;00m.$
   565^I$
   566^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m100[39;49;00m-[31mInitialization[39;49;00m$
   567^I[37mGC0609[39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mSET[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m88[39;49;00m-[31mNot-Complete[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mTRUE[39;49;00m$
   568^I[37mGC0609[39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mUNTIL[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m88[39;49;00m-[31mComplete[39;49;00m$
   569^I[37mGC0609[39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m200[39;49;00m-[31mLet-User-Set-Switches[39;49;00m$
   570^I[37mGC0609[39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m210[39;49;00m-[31mRun-Compiler[39;49;00m$
   571^I[37mGC0410[39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mIF [39;49;00m([34m88[39;49;00m-[31mCompile-OK[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[35mOR[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m88[39;49;00m-[31mCompile-OK-Warn[39;49;00m)$
   572^I[37mGC0410[39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[35mAND [39;49;00m([31mS-XREF[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[35mNOT [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[31mSPACE[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[35mOR[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mS-SOURCE[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[35mNOT [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[31mSPACE[39;49;00m)$
   573^I[37mGC0410[39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m220[39;49;00m-[31mMake-Listing[39;49;00m$
   574^I[37mGC0410[39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mEND-IF[39;49;00m$
   575^I[37mGC0709[39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mIF  [39;49;00m([31mS-EXECUTE[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[35mNOT [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[31mSPACES[39;49;00m)$
   576^I[37mGC0709[39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[35mAND [39;49;00m([34m88[39;49;00m-[31mOutput-File-Avail[39;49;00m)$
   577^I[37mGC0609[39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m230[39;49;00m-[31mRun-Program[39;49;00m$
   578^I[37mGC0609[39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mEND-IF[39;49;00m$
   579^I[37mGC0609[39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mEND-PERFORM[39;49;00m$
   580^I[34m           [39;49;00m.$
   581^I$
   582^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m009[39;49;00m-[31mDone[39;49;00m.$
   583^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m900[39;49;00m-[31mTerminate[39;49;00m$
   584^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m.$
   585^I[37m      * -- Control will NOT return[39;49;00m$
   586^I[37m      /[39;49;00m$
   587^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m010[39;49;00m-[31mParse-Args[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mSECTION[39;49;00m.$
   588^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
   589^I[37m      ** Process a sequence of KEYWORD=VALUE items.  These are items **[39;49;00m$
   590^I[37m      ** specified on the command-line to provide the initial        **[39;49;00m$
   591^I[37m      ** options shown selected on the screen.  When integrating     **[39;49;00m$
   592^I[37m      ** OCic into an edirot or framework, include these switches on **[39;49;00m$
   593^I[37m      ** the ocic.exe command the editor/framework executes.  Any    **[39;49;00m$
   594^I[37m      ** underlined choice is the default value for that switch.     **[39;49;00m$
   595^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   596^I[37m      ** @CONFIG=BS2000|COBOL85|COBOL2002|DEFAULT|IBM|MF|MVS         **[39;49;00m$
   597^I[37m      **                                  =======                    **[39;49;00m$
   598^I[37m      ** This switch specifies the default cobc compiler configura-  **[39;49;00m$
   599^I[37m      ** tion file to be used                                        **[39;49;00m$
   600^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   601^I[37m      ** @DEBUG=YES|NO                                               **[39;49;00m$
   602^I[37m      **            ==                                               **[39;49;00m$
   603^I[37m      ** This switch specifies whether (YES) or not (NO) debugging   **[39;49;00m$
   604^I[37m      ** lines (those with a "D" in column 7) will be compiled.      **[39;49;00m$
   605^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   606^I[37m      ** @DLL=YES|NO                                                 **[39;49;00m$
   607^I[37m      **          ==                                                 **[39;49;00m$
   608^I[37m      ** Use this switch to force ALL compiled programs to be built  **[39;49;00m$
   609^I[37m      ** as DLLs ("@DLL=YES").  When main programs are built as DLLs **[39;49;00m$
   610^I[37m      ** they must be executed using the cobcrun utility.  When      **[39;49;00m$
   611^I[37m      ** "@DLL=NO" is in effect, main programs are generated as      **[39;49;00m$
   612^I[37m      ** actual "exe" files and only subprograms will be generated   **[39;49;00m$
   613^I[37m      ** as DLLs.                                                    **[39;49;00m$
   614^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   615^I[37m      ** @EXECUTE=YES|NO                                             **[39;49;00m$
   616^I[37m      **              ==                                             **[39;49;00m$
   617^I[37m      ** This switch specifies whether ("@EXECUTE=YES") or not       **[39;49;00m$
   618^I[37m      ** ("@EXECUTE=NO") the program will be executed after it is    **[39;49;00m$
   619^I[37m      ** successfully compiled.                                      **[39;49;00m$
   620^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   621^I[37m      ** @EXTRA=extra cobc argument(s)                               **[39;49;00m$
   622^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   623^I[37m      ** This switch allows you to specify additional cobc arguments **[39;49;00m$
   624^I[37m      ** that aren't managed by the other OC switches.  If used,     **[39;49;00m$
   625^I[37m      ** this must be the last switch specified on the command line, **[39;49;00m$
   626^I[37m      ** as everything that follows the "=" will be placed on the    **[39;49;00m$
   627^I[37m      ** cobc command generated by OC.                               **[39;49;00m$
   628^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   629^I[37m      ** @NOTRUNC=YES|NO                                             **[39;49;00m$
   630^I[37m      **          ===                                                **[39;49;00m$
   631^I[37m      ** This switch specifies whether (YES) or not (NO) the sup-    **[39;49;00m$
   632^I[37m      ** pression of binary field truncation will occur.  If a PIC   **[39;49;00m$
   633^I[37m      ** 99 COMP field (one byte of storage), for example, is given  **[39;49;00m$
   634^I[37m      ** the value 123, it may have its value truncated to 23 when   **[39;49;00m$
   635^I[37m      ** DISPLAYed.  Regardless of the NOTRUNC setting, internally   **[39;49;00m$
   636^I[37m      ** the full precision of the field (allowing a maximum value   **[39;49;00m$
   637^I[37m      ** of 255) will be preserved.  Even though truncation - if it  **[39;49;00m$
   638^I[37m      ** does occur - would appear to have a minimal disruption on   **[39;49;00m$
   639^I[37m      ** program operation, it has a significant effect on program   **[39;49;00m$
   640^I[37m      ** run-time speed.                                             **[39;49;00m$
   641^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   642^I[37m      ** @TRACE=YES|NO|ALL                                           **[39;49;00m$
   643^I[37m      **            ==                                               **[39;49;00m$
   644^I[37m      ** This switch controls whether or not code will be added to   **[39;49;00m$
   645^I[37m      ** the object program to produce execution-time logic traces.  **[39;49;00m$
   646^I[37m      ** A specification of "@TRACE=NO" means no such code will be   **[39;49;00m$
   647^I[37m      ** produced.  By specifying "@TRACE=YES", code will be genera- **[39;49;00m$
   648^I[37m      ** ted to display procedure names as they are entered.  A      **[39;49;00m$
   649^I[37m      ** "@TRACE=ALL" specification will generate not only procedure **[39;49;00m$
   650^I[37m      ** traces (as "@TRACE=YES" would) but also statement-level     **[39;49;00m$
   651^I[37m      ** traces too!  All trace output is written to STDERR, so      **[39;49;00m$
   652^I[37m      ** adding a "2>file" to the execution of the program will pipe **[39;49;00m$
   653^I[37m      ** the trace output to a file.  You may find it valuable to    **[39;49;00m$
   654^I[37m      ** add your own DISPLAY statements to the debugging output via **[39;49;00m$
   655^I[37m      ** "DISPLAY xx UPON SYSERR"  The SYSERR device corresponds to  **[39;49;00m$
   656^I[37m      ** the Windows or UNIX STDERR device and will therefore honor  **[39;49;00m$
   657^I[37m      ** any "2>file" placed at the end of your program's execution. **[39;49;00m$
   658^I[37m      ** Add a "D" in column 7 and you can control the generation or **[39;49;00m$
   659^I[37m      ** ignoring of these DISPLAY statements via the "@DEBUG"       **[39;49;00m$
   660^I[37m      ** switch.                                                     **[39;49;00m$
   661^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   662^I[37mGC0410** @SOURCE=YES|NO                                              **[39;49;00m$
   663^I[37mGC0410**           ==                                                **[39;49;00m$
   664^I[37mGC0410** Use this switch to produce a source listing of the program, **[39;49;00m$
   665^I[37mGC0410** PROVIDED it compiles without errors.                        **[39;49;00m$
   666^I[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m$
   667^I[37mGC0410** @XREF=YES|NO                                                **[39;49;00m$
   668^I[37mGC0410**           ==                                                **[39;49;00m$
   669^I[37mGC0410** Use this switch to produce a cross-reference listing of the **[39;49;00m$
   670^I[37mGC0410** program, PROVIDED it compiles without errors.               **[39;49;00m$
   671^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
   672^I$
   673^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m011[39;49;00m-[31mInit[39;49;00m.$
   674^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mMOVE[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1 [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mI[39;49;00m$
   675^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m.$
   676^I$
   677^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m012[39;49;00m-[31mExtract-Kwd-And-Value[39;49;00m.$
   678^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mUNTIL[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mI[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[35mNOT [39;49;00m<[37m [39;49;00m[34mLENGTH[39;49;00m([31mCommand-Line-Args[39;49;00m)$
   679^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mMOVE[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mI[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mJ[39;49;00m$
   680^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mUNSTRING[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mCommand-Line-Args[39;49;00m$
   681^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[34mDELIMITED[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mBY[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mALL SPACES[39;49;00m$
   682^I[31m                  [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mINTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword-And-Value[39;49;00m$
   683^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[34mWITH[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mPOINTER[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mI[39;49;00m$
   684^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mEND-UNSTRING[39;49;00m$
   685^I[34m              [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mIF[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword-And-Value[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[35mNOT [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[31mSPACES[39;49;00m$
   686^I[31m                  [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mUNSTRING[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword-And-Value[39;49;00m$
   687^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                 [39;49;00m[34mDELIMITED[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mBY [39;49;00m[33m'='[39;49;00m$
   688^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                 [39;49;00m[34mINTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword[39;49;00m,[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Value[39;49;00m$
   689^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[34mEND-UNSTRING[39;49;00m$
   690^I[34m                  [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m030[39;49;00m-[31mProcess-Keyword[39;49;00m$
   691^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mEND-IF[39;49;00m$
   692^I[34m          [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mEND-PERFORM[39;49;00m$
   693^I[34m           [39;49;00m.$
   694^I$
   695^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m019[39;49;00m-[31mDone[39;49;00m.$
   696^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mEXIT[39;49;00m.$
   697^I$
   698^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
   699^I[37m      ** Since this program uses the SCREEN SECTION, it cannot do    **[39;49;00m$
   700^I[37m      ** conventional console DISPLAY operations.  This routine      **[39;49;00m$
   701^I[37m      ** (which, I admit, is like using an H-bomb to hunt rabbits)   **[39;49;00m$
   702^I[37m      ** will submit an "ECHO" command to the system to simulate a   **[39;49;00m$
   703^I[37m      ** DISPLAY.                                                    **[39;49;00m$
   704^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
   705^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m021[39;49;00m-[31mBuild-And-Issue-Command[39;49;00m.$
   706^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mDISPLAY[39;49;00m$
   707^I[34m              [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mOutput-Message[39;49;00m$
   708^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mEND-DISPLAY[39;49;00m$
   709^I[34m           [39;49;00m.$
   710^I$
   711^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m029[39;49;00m-[31mDone[39;49;00m.$
   712^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mEXIT[39;49;00m.$
   713^I[37m      /[39;49;00m$
   714^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m030[39;49;00m-[31mProcess-Keyword[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mSECTION[39;49;00m.$
   715^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
   716^I[37m      ** Process a single KEYWORD=VALUE item.                        **[39;49;00m$
   717^I[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m$
   718^I$
   719^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m031[39;49;00m-[31mInit[39;49;00m.$
   720^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mMOVE[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[32mUPPER-CASE[39;49;00m([31mSwitch-Keyword[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword[39;49;00m$
   721^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mSET[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m88[39;49;00m-[31mSwitch-Is-Good[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mTRUE[39;49;00m$
   722^I[36m           [39;49;00m.$
   723^I$
   724^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m032[39;49;00m-[31mProcess[39;49;00m.$

  1768^I[37m      **                             whether or not an xref listing  **[39;49;00m$
  1769^I[37m      **                             should be produced (space=NO,   **[39;49;00m$
  1770^I[37m      **                             non-space=yes)                  **[39;49;00m$
  1771^I[37m      **                  <filename> is the [path]filename of the    **[39;49;00m$
  1772^I[37m      **                             program being listed and/or     **[39;49;00m$
  1773^I[37m      **                             xreffed in a PIC X(256) form.   **[39;49;00m$
